// Added for identifying the international URLS
function parseURL( name )
{
  name = name.replace(/[\[]/,"\\\[").replace(/[\]]/,"\\\]");
  var regexS = "[\\?&]"+name+"=([^&#]*)";
  var regex = new RegExp( regexS );
  var results = regex.exec( windUrl );
  if( results == null )
    return "";
  else
    return results[1];
}
//Replaces the special characters with corresponding escape characters. 
 function cleanFilterParam(inputString) { 		 	
 	/*Replace all '%3F' characters with '?' */
 	while(inputString.indexOf('%3F')>=0){
 		inputString=inputString.replace('%3F','?');
 	}

 	/*Replace all '%3D' characters with '=' */
 	while(inputString.indexOf('%3D')>=0){
 		inputString=inputString.replace('%3D','=');
 	}

 	/*Replace all '%u2122' characters with '%26%23153%3B' */
 	while(inputString.indexOf('%u2122')>=0){
 		//inputString=inputString.replace('%u2122','%26%23153%3B');
 		inputString=inputString.replace('%u2122','%E2%84%A2');
 	}

 	/*Replace all '%AE' characters with '%26reg%3B' */
 	while(inputString.indexOf('%AE')>=0){
 		inputString=inputString.replace('%AE','%26reg%3B');
 	}
 	/*Replace all '%252B' characters with '%2B' */
 	while(inputString.indexOf('%252B')>=0){
 		inputString=inputString.replace('%252B','%2B');
 	}
 	return inputString;
 }

  <script>
					var SYWR_DOLLARS_SPENT = '0.10';
					var SYWR_POINTS_OBTAINED = '1';
					var SYWR_DOLLARS_SPENT_THRESHOLD = '0.05';
					var SYWR_DOLLAR_REWARD = '0.01';
					var SYWR_BASE_POINTS = '10';
					var SYWR_REDEMPTION_VALUE = '10';
					var LOYALTY_PINLESS_SERVICE = '';

					function calculatePoints(amountSpent){
						//calculate points from dollars spent
						amountSpent = Math.round(amountSpent*100*100)/100;
						var baseVal = SYWR_DOLLARS_SPENT*100;
						var modVal = amountSpent%baseVal;
						var points = Math.floor(amountSpent/baseVal)*SYWR_POINTS_OBTAINED;
						var roundUpFactor = SYWR_DOLLARS_SPENT_THRESHOLD*100;
						if(modVal >= roundUpFactor){
							points = points + parseInt(SYWR_POINTS_OBTAINED);
						}
						return points;
					}

Products over 35lbs cannot be shipped to APO/FPO locations - all APO/FPO shipments are USPS. Estimated offer value ranges from $6.80 to $64. Offer excludes shipping costs on Oversized Shipping or In-Home Oversized Shipping Items.</p>
